2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 To enable it, first install UCX (conda install -c conda-forge ucx).
2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 Afterwards, set the environment variables
2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 OMPI_MCA_pml=ucx OMPI_MCA_osc=ucx
2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 before launching your MPI processes.
2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameters in the command line:
2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 mpiexec --mca pml ucx --mca osc ucx ...
2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 
2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6

2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 OMPI_MCA_coll_ucc_enable=1

2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2024-10-21T21:07:19Z #11 259.6 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
